 People visiting the country's first 'seeing in the Dark' restaurant-theater in Vastrapur area of ahmedabad can experience life without light like blind people where darkness is spread all around
 blind pipuls association dwaara haal main banaae is jagah par deevaaren, farsh, parde, mej or kursiyaan, asi or pankhe sabhi kaale rang se range hai or yahaan aane vaale logon ke liye roshni kii koi gunjaaish nahin he
 In this restaurant you will have to come to your table, grope in the dark, order your food and eat without lights
 aapako yahaan apni plate bamushkil hi dikhaai degi, usamen rakhe lajij vyanjanon kii to alag baat he
 Here you can also enjoy the film in a dark black theater with a seating capacity of 50 people
 bipie kii nideshak nandani rawal kahati hai, 'yah vichaar koi nayaa nahin he
 There are such restaurants in Western countries
 hamane vahaan se yah idia liya lekin bharat main is kism kaa yah pehla restaraan hai
 He said, 'our motive is double
 jis samaaj main ham dekh rahe hai ki dusron ke prati samvednaaen kam ho raheen hai, aise main ham chaahate hai ki logon ko is cheez kaa anubhav ho ki bina najaron ke jindagi kisi hoti he
 This can increase understanding towards people who do not have light in their eyes
 'nandani ne kaha, 'doosraa makasad he ki hamaare jaise log, jinhen saare sakriy ang uphaar main mili hai, ham un logon ko halke main lete hai' ‚Äòseeing in dark‚Äô yani andhere main dekhne ke ehsaas ke saath ham un logon kii tarif karenge or ishwar kaa shukriya adaa karenge ki hamaare sabhi ang acchhee haalat main hai

 co / wa9vkda8b8 aaj deshbhar menkarava chouth(karwa Chauth 2018) kii dhooma he
 Karwa Chauth 2018, celebrated on the Chaturthi of Kartik Krishna Paksha, is special for women
 pati or patni kaa rishta sabase bada or pavitra rishta mana jaataa he or isi rishte ko majboot karne ke liye hi karvaa chouth kaa tyohaar manaaya jaataa he
 In Karva Chauth, women observe this fast for the long life of their husband and their well wishes
 mitti ke totinuma paatr jisase jal arpit karte hai, uskokarwakaha jaataa he
 On Karva Chauth, women break their vow only after drinking water from an earthen carve
 isliye karvaa chouth par jitna mahatv chalni kaa hota he, utana hi karave kaa bhi hota he
 But have you wondered why the Suhagin women break their fast by drinking water from Karve on the day of Karva Chauth, let us know
 
 
 ye he mitti ke karave kaa mahatv-darasal, karave ko banane ke liye sabase pehlemittike saath pani milaayaa jaataa he, jo jal or bhoomi tatv ke pratik hai
 After making the Karve, it is dried by placing it in the sun and air, which are the symbols of the sky and air element
 iske baad karave ko aag main tapaaya jaataa he, is tarah karvaa paanch tatwon se milakar banataa he
 Hence Karve is considered a symbol of the five elements
 in paanch tatwon kii madad se bane hone ke kaaran mitti ke karave kaa mahatv steneles steel se bane karave ke mukaable adhik hota he
 This is the reason why the husband ends the fast of Karva Chauth by watering his wife with an earthen pot, so that he can wish the five elements in his married life a happy life
 iske alaava ayurveda main bhi mitti ke bartan se pani pine ko sehat ke liye acha bataaya gaya he, lekin aadhunik jivan main aajkal kuch log mitti ke karave kii jagah steneles steel ke karave kaa bhi istemaal karne lage hai
